TB Resolution 2025-496 
 
APPROVES FIREWORKS PERMIT FOR THE ROCK GOLF CLUB (JULY 5, 2025) 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, The Rock Golf Club had submitted a Fireworks Permit Application 
for the purpose of conducting a fireworks display at 141 Fairway Drive, Wading River, 
New York on July 5, 2025, at approximately 9:00 p.m.; and  
 
WHEREAS, the $500.00 administrative fee has been paid to the Office of the 
Fire Marshal; and the $200.00 Fireworks Permit Application fee has been paid. 
 
WHEREAS, the Town Clerk is in receipt of a completed Fireworks Application 
executed by the Chief of the Fire Department and the Riverhead Fire Marshal and a 
certificate of insurance from the fireworks company (Fireworks by Santore’s World 
Famous Fireworks LLC) naming the Town of Riverhead as an additional insured in 
respect of liability caused by the negligent acts or omissions and has determined that 
same is satisfactory as to their form.  
 
WHEREAS, Notification to all horse farms located within a half mile radius must 
be notified via certified mail of the fireworks display.  Certified mail receipts and a copy 
of the notification letter must be presented to the fire marshal no later than five days 
prior to the display 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Fireworks Permit Application of 
The Rock Golf Club for the purpose of conducting a fireworks display is hereby 
approved with the following conditions: 
 
 The required fire suppression equipment and personnel shall be provided by 
the Fire Department. 
 Scheduling a pre-event inspection between 12:00 noon and 2:00 p.m. on the 
day of the event having the Fireworks technician(s), the Riverhead Fire 
Marshal and the Fire Chief in attendance. 
 Fireworks and technicians must arrive at the site no later than 2:00 p.m. on 
the day of the event. 
 Fire Marshal to be present 30 minutes prior to commencement of show for 
purpose of final inspection and safety review. 
 The show shall be limited to firework shells as listed on the Fireworks Permit 
application. 
 The Fire Marshal shall have the final authorization to allow the show to 
proceed or cancel the show if there are unsafe conditions, lightning and/or 
wind in excess of 30 miles per hour; and be it further  
  
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby authorized to forward a copy of this 
9.30
Packet Pg. 199
resolution to Chief of Police, Edward Frost, Chief Fire Marshal, Andrew Smith, Chris 
Vene chris@baitinghollowclub.com, Santore’s Famous Fireworks 
terisa@santorefireworks.com, and Wading River Fire District chiefs@wadingriverfd.org; 
and be it further 
 
 
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a copy of same may be 
obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.   
 
 
THE VOTE

River, New York, at specific locations as outlined on the attached map (Schedule “A”); 
and 
 
WHEREAS, the Samantha Nagorski has requested permission to allow alcohol 
service within the licensed premises at the subject place, date and time; and 
 
WHEREAS, North Fork Brewing Company, LLC will be the only designated 
alcohol service vendor for participation regarding the subject event. 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED , that the Town of Riverhead approves 
North Fork Brewing Company, LLC as the alcohol service vendor at the “DUCK POND 
DAY” on Sunday, June 8, 2025 from 9:00 a.m. to 6:00 p.m., at the Town of Riverhead’s 
property located at 1016 North Country Road, Wading River, New York, described 
hereinafter as the “Licensed Area” as outlined on the attached map (Schedule “A”) 
subject to the following conditions: 
 
1. Each participating alcohol service vendor shall comply with New York State 
Alcohol Beverage Control Laws, NYS Liquor Authority Rules and 
Regulations and the Town of Riverhead Alcohol Policy, as applicable. 
 
2. Each participating alcohol service vendor shall execute a license 
agreement in a form to be approved by the Town Attorney’s Office. 
 
3. Each participating alcohol service vendor shall procure a general liability 
insurance policy for the subject activity naming the Town of Riverhead and 
Polish Town Civic Association, as “additional insureds” on a primary and 
non-contributory basis , with policy limits of at least $1,000,000 per 
occurrence/ $2,000,000 aggregate, including food/product service liability 
protection, if applicable.  In addition to the above referenced insurance 
requirements, alcohol vendors shall also procure an additional insurance 
liability policy regarding alcohol service liability with policy limits of at 
least $2,000,000.00 dollars per occurrence/$2,000,000.00 dollars aggregate 
which shall name the above -referenced parties as additional insureds also 
on a primary and non-contributory basis. 
9.31
Packet Pg. 202
 
4.  Alcohol service shall also be subject to the following conditions: 
 
a. All alcohol servers must be TIPS (Training for Intervention Procedures) 
approved by New York State. 
b. Alcohol service and consumption shall be limited to the authorized and 
approved alcohol service vendors named herein as limited to the 
licensed premises (as delineated on the Riverhead Country Fair map), 
as follows. 
c. Alcohol service shall be solely limited to beer, cider, wine and/or 
champagne.   
d. Alcohol service shall be limited to two (2) drinks per age -appropriate -
customer at a time. 
e. Licensee shall possess and provide, prior to participation, a valid New 
York State Liquor Authority catering permit, or other appropriate permit, 
regarding off -premises alcohol service and comply with all applicable 
permit requirements including all other applicable municipal laws, rules 
and regulations, including service hours. 
f. Alcohol service shall be served in clear plastic cups or glass mugs and 
contain an identifying symbol and/or logo uniquely identifying the 
vendor. Each such cup shall be limited in size to 12 oz. for beer/cider; 5 
oz. for wine/champagne. 
g. Alcohol servers must personally affix wristbands to the wrists of age -
appropriate customers in a manner that prevents easy removal and 
transferability, no exceptions.   
h. Such other conditions more fully delineated in the alcohol vendor 
license agreement and Town of Riverhead Alcohol Policy; and be it 
further, 
 
RESOLVED, that the Riverhead Town Code §205 -3, which prohibits the 
consumption of any alcoholic beverages in any public place within the Town of 
Riverhead and also prohibits the possession of any open or unsealed container of an 
alcoholic beverage while in a public place for the purposes of consumption, is hereby 
suspended for enforcement purposes solely regarding “DUCK POND DAY” on Sunday, 
June 8, 2025 from 9:00 a.m. to 6:00 p.m., at the Town of Riverhead’s property located 
at 1016 North Country Road, Wading River, New York, as outlined on the attached map 
(Schedule “A”), subject to the above -stated requirements, solely limited to the licensed 
premises as delineated on Schedule “A” and subject to the New York State Alcohol 
Beverage Control Law and NYS Liquor Authority Rules and Regulations; and it be 
further,

Chapter 105 Boards, Commissions and Councils 
 
Article XVIII Traffic Violations Bureau: Liability for Failure to 
Stop for School Buses 
 
 
§ 105-81 Purpose. 
§ 105-83 Hearing before administrative law judge. 
§ 105-84 Jurisdiction. 
§ 105-85 Authorization of program. 
§ 105-86 Costs of program. 
§ 105-87 Vehicle owner liability for operator violations. 
§ 105-88 Adjudication of liability. 
§ 105-89 Payment of fines without court appearance. 
§ 105-90 Penalties for offenses. 
 
 
§ 105-81 Purpose. 
In order to provide additional protection to school -aged children boarding and de -boarding 
school buses that are legally stopped upon highways and roads while engaging in 
transportation services, the State of New York  imposed liability on the owners of motor 
vehicles for failing to stop when school buses display red visual signals and the bus stop-arm 
is deployed. The Town of Riverhead hereby enacts this chapter in order to ratify procedures 
for adjudication of VTL 1174-a liability notices. 
 
§ 105-82 Definitions. 
As used in this chapter, the following terms shall have the meanings indicated: 
 
ADMINISTRATIVE LAW JUDGE 
A lawyer qualified and appointed by the Riverhead Town Board for the limited purpose of 
conducting administrative hearings and adjudicating VTL 1174 -a liability notices following 
such hearings. 
 
COUNTY 
County of Suffolk. 
 
MANUAL ON UNIFORM TRAFFIC CONTROL DEVICES OR MUTCD 
The manual and specifications for a uniform system of traffic control devices maintained 
pursuant to NYS VTL § 1680. 
 
NYS VTL 
New York State Vehicle and Traffic Law. 
 
OWNER 
Shall have the meaning provided in NYS VTL § 239. 
 
9.32.a
Packet Pg. 209
Attachment: Chapter 105 Bus Liability  (2025-498 : Authorizes Town Clerk to Publish and Post Public Notice to Consider a Local Law to Amend
RECORDED IMAGES AND DATA 
Photographs, microphotographs, videotapes, other recorded images or data created with 
respect to the program authorized by this chapter. 
 
SCHOOL BUS PHOTO VIOLATION MONITORING SYSTEM 
A device that is capable of operating independently of an operator or enforcement officer, 
specifically installed to work in conjunction with a school bus stop -arm, which device when 
triggered produces records of images of a vehicle being used or operated in violation of NYS 
VTL § 1174-a. 
 
§ 105-83 Hearing before administrative law judge. 
An administrative law judge/s designated by the Justice Court to conduct and adjudicate VTL 
1174-a notices of liability. Such hearings shall take place at a Town facility outside of the 
Riverhead Town Justice Court during the same hours as the Justice Court. Hearings may be 
conducted virtually. Nothing contained within this chapter shall authorize an administrative 
law judge operating under the authority of the Traffic Violation Bureau to deprive a person of 
their right to counsel, or prevent a person from exercising their right to appear to answer to, 
explain, or defend any charge of violation of NYS VTL § 1174-a. An administrative law judge 
shall not have the power to issue a warrant. An administ rative law judge shall not set any 
form of bail in any instance. 
 
§ 105-84 Jurisdiction. 
An administrative law judge/s designated by the Town Board to conduct and adjudicate VTL 
1174-a notices of liability shall only have jurisdiction to hold hearings for such purpose for the 
Town of Riverhead, pursuant to a duly executed intermunicipal agreement conferring such 
jurisdiction upon the Town Board’s designated administrative law judge/s. 
 
§ 105-85 Authorization of program. 
Pursuant to the authorization provided by NYS VTL §  1174-a, there is hereby established a 
program imposing monetary liability on owners of vehicles where operators of the owner's 
vehicle violate NYS VTL § 1174-a. 
 
§ 105-86 Costs of program. 
A. The total cost to the school district of the installation, maintenance and use of school bus 
photo violation monitoring systems pursuant to an agreement authorized by this chapter 
shall be borne entirely by the county/school district. 
B.  Any cost or expense not addressed by NYS VTL § 1174-a, Subdivision (a)1-b, shall be 
allocated by agreement, or as otherwise required by law. 
 
§ 105-87 Vehicle owner liability for operator violations. 
A.  Subject to the procedures, rules and standards of conduct set forth in NYS VTL § 1174-
a, the owner of a vehicle shall be liable for a penalty imposed pursuant to this chapter if the 
owner's vehicle was used or operated with the permission of the owner, express or implied, 
in violation of NYS VTL § 1174-a. 
B. The Riverhead Town Police Department shall review allegations of violations from the 
school districts with whom the county contracts under this program. 
(1) The Riverhead Town Police Department may contract with a nonmunicipal entity to 
formulate notices that contain the content required by NYS VTL § 1174-a, Subdivision (g). 
9.32.a
Packet Pg. 210
Attachment: Chapter 105 Bus Liability  (2025-498 : Authorizes Town Clerk to Publish and Post Public Notice to Consider a Local Law to Amend
The contracted nonmunicipal entity shall take such steps as necessary to ensure notices 
are delivered in the manner described in NYS VTL § 1174-a, Subdivision (g). 
 
 
§ 105-88 Adjudication of liability. 
Where an operator of a vehicle violates the standards set forth in NYS VTL §  1174-a, 
Subdivision (b), liability may be imposed upon a vehicle owner by a Town Board appointed 
administrative law judge, as designated by the court, and serving the court of com petent 
jurisdiction that has jurisdiction over the location where the violation occurred in the manner, 
and upon the proof permitted by, NYS VTL §  1174-a, or in any other manner or other proof 
permitted by law. An administrative law judge shall only have j urisdiction to find a vehicle 
"liable" or "not liable" for an alleged offense of NYS VTL § 1174-a. An administrative law judge 
may not engage in any plea bargaining or render any decision outside of a determination of 
"liable" or "not liable." 
 
§ 105-89 Payment of fines without court appearance. 
An owner of a vehicle who has received a notice of liability charging NYS VTL §  1174-a, 
within the time specified in said notice, may answer online (website address must be provided 
upon the notice of liability) writing, waiving a hearing in court, pleading guilty to the charge 
pay the applicable fine. Acceptance of the prescribed fine shall be deemed complete 
satisfaction for the violation, and the violator shall be given a receipt. 
 
§ 105-90 Penalties for offenses. 
A.  An owner liable for a violation of this chapter shall be liable for those monetary penalties 
set forth in NYS VTL § 1174-a, Subdivision (e); and fines shall be paid. Payment 
instructions shall be provided upon the notice of liability. 
B.  An additional penalty for each violation for the failure to respond to a notice of liability 
within the prescribed time period. 
C.  For purpose of this chapter, there is a rebuttable presumption that a vehicle was used 
and operated with the consent of the owner at the time it was used and operated in violation 
of NYS VTL § 1174-a. 
D. If the owner receives a notice of liability pursuant to this chapter for a violation, it shall be 
a valid defense that the alleged violation took place at a time during which the vehicle was 
reported to the police as having been stolen and that the vehicle had been reported to the 
police as stolen prior to the time the violation occurred and had not been recovered by such 
time. For purposes of asserting the defense provided by this subsection, it shall be sufficient 
that a certified copy of the police report on the stolen vehicle be sent or delivered to a court 
of competent jurisdiction or parking violations bureau having jurisdiction where any 
contested notice of liability would otherwise be determined. 
E. No owner of a vehicle shall be liable for a penalty imposed pursuant to this chapter 
where the operator of such vehicle has been convicted of the underlying violation of NYS 
VTL § 1174-a. 
 
 
9.32.a
Packet Pg. 211
Attachment: Chapter 105 Bus Liability  (2025-498 : Authorizes Town Clerk to Publish and Post Public Notice to Consider a Local Law to Amend
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD  
NOTICE OF PUBLIC HEARING  
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board of the 
Town of Riverhead at Riverhead Town Hall, 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York, on the 
1st day of July, 2025 at or about 2:20 p.m. to amend Chapter 105 of the Riverhead Town Code 
Titled “Boards, Commissions, and Councils”, Article XVII thereof titled, “Traffic Violations Bureau: 
Liability for Failure to Stop for School Buses”  
 
The intent of the proposed legislation is to create a venue to adjudicate cases specific to 
school bus arm cameras which are otherwise unable to be heard in the Town Justice Court.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
PUBLIC NOTICE 
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead adopted a 
resolution setting forth findings and determinations relative to 127 East Main Street and SNR Bar 
25 Corp.’s Leasehold Interest therein.  
 
Pursuant to Article 2 of the Eminent Domain Procedure Law, a public hearing regarding 
the acquisition of SNR Bar 25 Corp.’s Leasehold Interest to the easterly ground floor rental unit 
located at 127 East Main Street, Riverhead, New York, 11901, Suffolk County Tax Map #600-
129-1-14, was held by the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead on May 21, 2025 to inform the 
public and to review the public use to be served by the acquisition and to review the impact of the 
acquisition on the community. 
 
On the 3rd day of June, 2025, the condemnor made its findings and determinations based 
on the hearing.  A copy of the findings and determination will be forwarded to any interested 
person without cost upon written request to the Clerk of the Town of Riverhead, 4 West Second 
Street, Riverhead, New York, 11901. 
 
A synopsis of the findings and determinations is as follows: 
 
 The Town Board of the Town of Riverhead has found and determined that the acquisition 
of the parcel listed below will benefit the public and will be for general municipal purposes as 
part of the overall Town Square Project, which includes the 127 East Main Street property. 
 
The property to be acquired is commonly known as SNR Bar 25 Corp.’s Leasehold 
Interest to the easterly ground floor rental unit located at 127 East Main Street, Riverhead, New 
York, 11901, (Suffolk County Tax Map #600-129-1-14). 
 
After review of the SEQRA record, the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead, as lead 
agency, has determined that this acquisition, as part of the overall Town Square project, is not 
expected to result in any significant adverse environmental impacts. 
 
A copy of the entire text of the above resolution may be reviewed at the Office of the 
Town Clerk, 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York 11901, between the hours of 8:30 a.m. 
and 4:30 p.m., Monday through Friday and can be accessed on the Town of Riverhead website at: 
www.townofriverheadny.gov under the Agenda and Minutes for the June 3, 2025 Town Board 
Meeting.

WHEREAS, in a memo dated April 30, 2025, the Chief Fire Marshal had the 
following comments: 
 
1. Gates must be compliant with Town Code and have emergency access 
features. 
 
§231-64 Security Gates 
 
A. The installation of security gates across an emergency vehicle access road 
shall comply with the provisions of the Fire Code of New York State.  Access 
shall be provided for emergency vehicles as follows, and same requires the 
approval of the Fire Chief and Fire Marshal. 
 
B. Security gate required features. 
 
1. Access gate shall be provided with a keypad entry system. 
 
2. Coded numbers will be designated by the Fire Chief and Police Chief for 
Fire, Ambulance, and Police Department emergency access. 
 
3. All access gates shall be designed to unlock with a readily accessible 
manual releasing device and be capable of being locked open during an 
emergency. 
 
4. During a power failure, all access gates shall be designed to fail in the 
open position. 
 
5. A Knox key box shall be installed at the gate in all gated communities. 
 
6. Access gates shall not obstruct the required minimum Fire Department 
access road; and  
 
WHEREAS¸ in an email dated April 30, 2025, the Riverhead Highway 
Superintendent had the following comments: 
 
I am requiring any openings of the road in that area to be fully restored curb to curb.  
The Highway Department just paved that intersection from State Road 25 north; and 
 
WHEREAS, the subject property is located within the New York State 
Department of Environmental Conservation’s Wild, Scenic, and Recreational Rivers 
area (Community designation); and  
  
 WHEREAS, pursuant to 6NYCRR Part 666.13(H)(1) and (2), no permit is 
required from the NYSDEC for the proposed improvements; and  
 
 WHEREAS¸ in an email dated April 24, 2025, the Riverhead Water District 
indicated that the hydrant located on the east side of Mill Road, which is to be relocated 
in order to construct the new access driveway, is owned by the Riverhead Water 
District, and that the hydrant must remain on the east side of Mill Road; and  
 
WHEREAS, the Town Board has considered the criteria for Special Permit 
consideration, as enumerated in Town Code §301-312 A-R; and  
9.34
Packet Pg. 218
 
WHEREAS, the Town Board has considered the report of the Planning 
Department, comments received at the public hearing, the SEQRA record to date, as 
well as other relevant planning, zoning, and environmental factors.  Now, therefore be it 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Board hereby determines the following: 
 
1. That the use will not prevent or substantially impair either the reasonable and 
orderly use or the reasonable and orderly development of other properties in 
the neighborhood. 
 
2. That the hazards or disadvantages to the neighborhood from the location of 
such use at the property are outweighed by the advantage to be gained either 
by the neighborhood or the Town. 
 
3. The health, safety, welfare, comfort, convenience and order of the Town will 
not be adversely affected by the authorized use. 
 
4. That such use will be in harmony with and promote the general purposes and 
intent of Chapter 301 of the Riverhead Town Code; and be it further

Grid Facility Upgrades, subject to the following conditions:

plan approval from the Riverhead Planning Board and satisfy any and all 
conditions of site plan approval; and be it further

complete construction and begin this specially permitted use within three years of the

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-501 
 
RATIFIES AUTHORIZATION FOR THE TOWN ATTORNEY TO EXECUTE AN 
AGREEMENT WITH JEFFREY SEEMAN FOR SEQRA REVIEW 
 
Councilwoman Merrifield offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Waski 
 
WHEREAS, the Town Board desires to retain and enter into a professional 
services agreement with Jeffrey Seeman, Certified Environmental Professional, for 
expert and consulting services related to the Suffolk County Water Authority’s proposed 
“North Fork Transmission Line” comprising of a watermain extension from Flanders to 
Southold, NY; and 
 
 WHEREAS, Suffolk County Water Authority has commenced environmental 
review for the project and identified the Town of Riverhead as an “interested” agency 
rather than an “involved” agency despite substantial construction within the Town of 
Riverhead or upon Town of Riverhead Highways requiring road opening permits and 
easements and the proposed construction of a booster station on Pier Avenue requiring 
Town of Riverhead building permits and other services; and 
 
 WHEREAS, the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead objects to the designation 
of the Town of Riverhead as an “interested” agency instead of an “involved” agency and 
believes it to be crucial that Mr. Seeman, together with relevant Town Departments, 
advocate for the Town’s interests and jurisdictional authority through the Scoping 
process for the DEIS associated with the project.  
 
 NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED , that the Town Board hereby retains 
Jeffrey Seeman, Certified Environmental Professional, at a fee $165.00 per hour (not 
exceeding $5,000.00 for all services described and set forth in a Professional Services 
Agreement; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Board hereby ratifies authorization for the Town 
Attorney to execute a Professional Services Agreement with Jeffrey Seeman, Certified 
Environmental Professional; and be it further, 
 
 RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the Office of the Town Attorney and the Financial Administrator; and be it 
further 
 
 RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

LICENSE AGREEMENT 
 
 
 This Contract is made and entered into as of this _____ day of May, 2025, by and 
between Civil Air Patrol, 9th Suffolk Cadet Squadron, an duly authorized unit of the United 
States Air Force Auxiliary, Civil Air Patrol, National Headquarters, 105 S. Hansell Street, 
Bldg. 714, Maxwell AFB, AL 36112 (“Civil Air Patrol”) and the T own of Riverhead 
Community Development Agency (sometimes “CDA”), a urban renewal agency, with 
offices located at 4 West Second Street, Town of Riverhead, County of Suffolk and State 
of New York: 
 WHEREAS, Civil Air Patrol wishes to utilize specified locations located within 
property owned by the CDA and for the purposes of launching model rockets in 
connection with its classroom instruction curriculum; and  
 WHEREAS, the CDA has agreed to permit the utilization for said production at the 
following locations: 
 Enterprise Park at Calverton.  On an unobstructed area upon the southern portion 
of the 7,000-foot western runway/taxiway. 
 WHEREAS, Civil Air Patrol has agreed to terms under which it will be granted the 
use of said locations; 
 NOW THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants hereinafter set forth, 
the parties agree as follows: 
1. Use of Property: The CDA hereby grants Civil Air Patrol permission to utilize the 
aforementioned location on June 28, 2025 from 10:00 a.m. to 1:00 p.m. with an agreed 
upon rain date of June 29, 2025 by the parties for the aforementioned purposes.  Civil Air 
Patrol shall have no access to the surrounding grasslands and shall ensure that 
participants do not enter upon or  otherwise traverse the grasslands except in furtherance 
of clean-up associated with the licensed activities.   
2.   Cleanup:  Civil Air Patrol agrees to provide cleanup, fire protection and removal of 
any and all materials, debris or props deposited by reason of its actions in connection 
with the Agreement.  
3. Compliance With Laws:    Civil Air Patrol, agrees at all times to comply with all 
applicable federal, state, county and municipal laws, regulations, ordinances, codes and 
9.36.a
Packet Pg. 226
Attachment: Civil Air Patrol Agreement 2025  (2025-502 : Authorizes Supervisor to Execute License Agreement with Civil Air Patrol, 9Th Suffolk
 2 
restrictions, including, without limitation, compliance with Article 28 of the New York State 
Tax Law and applicable regulations thereunder, and will secure any and all permits or 
licenses required for its activities and operations carried out at the locations. 
4. Compensation:   There is no compensation for the use of the aforementioned CDA 
location by Civil Air Patrol.  
5.  Responsibilities of Civil Air Patrol:    Subject to the terms of this Agreement, Civil 
Air Patrol will be responsible for carrying out and shall have exclusive control of all 
operations associated with the Event and related activities, including without limitation, 
and shall diligently and con tinuously engage in such cleanup efforts so that the cleanup 
will be accomplished as soon as reasonably practicable (but in no event later than two 
days thereafter).   All locations will be restored to the condition  that existed prior to the 
Event (hereafter, the "restoration") and be completely clean and free of clutter and debris.   
6. Insurance and Indemnification:   Civil Air Patrol will be responsible for providing 
comprehensive general liability insurance in the amount of not less than  $1,000,000 and 
automobile liability insurance coverage of not less than $1,000,000.00 with a company or 
companies reasonably satisfactory to the Town. Civil Air Patrol shall provide certificates 
of the foregoing insurance, showing the Town of Riverhead Com munity Development 
Agency and Town of Riverhead as additional insureds to the extent of their in terest.  
Finally, Civil Air Patrol agrees to indemnify and hold harmless the Town of Riverhead 
Community Development Agency and their respective officers, employees, agents, 
representatives and officials  from any and all loss or liability associated with the Events 
and related activities described herein, including liability for damages to property or for 
injuries or death to persons which may arise from, or be attributable or incident to the use 
by Civil Air Patrol and its employees, agents, representativ es and concessionaires,  of 
the aforementioned.  With respect to any suit or claim by the Town of Riverhead 
Community Development Agency, whether under this indemnification provision or 
otherwise, Bootleg Productions, Inc. for itself, its agents, employees and representatives, 
hereby expressly waives any defense which might preclude or limit either enforcement of 
this indemnification clause or any reasonable attorney’s fees incurred by the CDA 
securing compliance with the provision of this indemnification agreement. 
7. Successors and Assigns.  This agreement shall be binding upon and inure to the

benefit of the respective successors and assigns of the parties; provided, however, that 
nothing herein shall be deemed to permit the assignment of this Agreement by either 
party without the express written consent of the other party. 
8. Entire Agreement.  This contract constitutes the entire agreement between the 
parties and no further agreement, express or implied, written or oral, exists with respect 
to the subject matter of this document. 
9.     Governing Law .   This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in 
accordance with the laws of the State of New York.

AGREEMENT 
 
BETWEEN, THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD,  a municipal corporation with offices at 4 
West Second Street, Riverhead, New York, hereinafter referred to as "TOWN" and RONALD A. 
CORELLA, a Certified Spanish Interpreter, residing at 71 Tyler Drive, Riverhead, New York 
11901, hereinafter referred to as " CORELLA". 
 
W I T N E S S E T H 
WHEREAS, the Town, in connection with its municipal operations, requires services 
consisting of the following: Language Translation; and  
 
WHEREAS, CORELLA is willing to provide the following services to the Town: 
 
Description of Services:   Language Translation – Spanish 
Date(s) and Hours of Services: On-call, Flexible 
 
IT IS HEREBY AGREED, by the Town and CORELLA as follows: 
 
1. CORELLA shall provide and fully perform to the Town's satisfaction the 
aforementioned services to the Town on the date(s) and times(s) stated above. 
 
2. In return for CORELLA ’s services, the Town shall pay CORELLA  Per Diem 
Interpreter Rates as follows:  A full-day rate of Three Hundred Eighty-Five ($385.00) 
Dollars and a half -day rate (calculated work of four hours or less) in the amount of 
Two Hundred Twenty ($220.00) Dollars. That sum shall be payable after CORELLA 
performs the services described for the Town and after CORELLA  has filed with the 
Town of Riverhead, vouchers and any other documents reasonably required for 
payment. 
 
3. If a court interpreting assignment is canceled and CORELLA  is notified the Town 
shall pay the following cancelation rates: No fee shall be paid if  CORELLA is 
notified prior to the scheduled hour on the previous business day; within 3- 24 hours 
before the scheduled start  time of the assignment, half (50%) of the regular fee shall 
be paid. If the assignment was scheduled for a full day at $385, CORELLA  shall be 
paid $192.50 for the canceled assignment. If the assignment was for a half day at 
$220, CORELLA shall be paid $110 for the canceled assignment;  less than three (3) 
hours before the scheduled start time of the assignment , full fee shall be  paid. If the 
assignment was scheduled for a full day, CORELLA  shall be  paid $385. If the 
assignment was scheduled for a half day, CORELLA  shall be  paid $220. No 
cancelation fee shall be paid for administrative closings for reasons including 
inclement weather and emergencies. CORELLA  will be deemed "notified" of a 
cancellation when notice is sent by e -mail to the address on file with the  Riverhead 
Justice Court.  
 
WHEREAS, either party may terminate this agreement upon 30 days prior written 
notice; and  
 
WHEREAS, any previously executed agreements are hereby determined to be null and 
void; and

06.03.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-506 
 
APPROVES FIREWORKS PERMIT FOR DREAMLAND AMUSEMENTS (JUNE 28, 
2025) 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, Dreamland Amusements had submitted a Fireworks Permit 
Application for the purpose of conducting a fireworks display at Veterans Memorial 
Park, Calverton, New York on June 28, 2025, at approximately 9:45 p.m.; and  
 
WHEREAS, the $500.00 administrative fee has been paid to the Office of the 
Fire Marshal; and the $200.00 Fireworks Permit Application fee has been paid. 
 
WHEREAS, the Town Clerk is in receipt of a completed Fireworks Application 
executed by the Chief of the Fire Department and the Riverhead Fire Marshal and a 
certificate of insurance from the fireworks company (Fireworks by Grucci, Inc.) naming 
the Town of Riverhead as an additional insured in respect of liability caused by the 
negligent acts or omissions and has determined that same is satisfactory as to their 
form.  
 
WHEREAS, Notification to all horse farms located within a half mile radius must 
be notified via certified mail of the fireworks display.  Certified mail receipts and a copy 
of the notification letter must be presented to the fire marshal no later than five days 
prior to the display 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Fireworks Permit Application of 
Dreamland Amusements for the purpose of conducting a fireworks display is hereby 
approved with the following conditions: 
 
§ The required fire suppression equipment and personnel shall be provided by 
the Fire Department. 
§ Scheduling a pre-event inspection between 12:00 noon and 2:00 p.m. on the 
day of the event having the Fireworks technician(s), the Riverhead Fire 
Marshal and the Fire Chief in attendance. 
§ Fireworks and technicians must arrive at the site no later than 2:00 p.m. on 
the day of the event. 
§ Fire Marshal to be present 30 minutes prior to commencement of show for 
purpose of final inspection and safety review. 
§ The show shall be limited to firework shells as listed on the Fireworks Permit 
application. 
§ The Fire Marshal shall have the final authorization to allow the show to 
proceed or cancel the show if there are unsafe conditions, lightning and/or 
wind in excess of 30 miles per hour; and be it further

Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution,

Part-Time Bilingual Clerk in the Town Clerk’s Office; and 
 
WHEREAS, this vacancy was duly posted as Job Posting # 4 of 202 5, duly 
advertised, interviews were conducted, and as a result a recommendation of a suitable 
candidate has been received from the Personnel Committee. 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED that pending the results of a successfully 
completed background investigation and other necessary pre -employment screenings 
for this position, this Town Board hereby appoints Karina Rios to the position of Part-
Time Bilingual Clerk  effective June 16, 2025  and sets her salary at a rate of pay as 
$20.00 per hour.

resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same

06.03.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-508 
 
SETS HOURS FOR TOWN BEACH PARKING LOTS 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, Section 211-21 of the Riverhead Town Code directs the Town Board 
to establish the hours and period of time a public bathing beaches and town beach 
parking lots shall be open. 
  WHEREAS, public bathing beaches are defined as shoreline areas owned, 
maintained, or operated by the Town of Riverhead for the use and enjoyment of 
residents and visitors, which typically include designated swimming areas with 
appropriate safety measures, lifeguards on duty during operating hours, parking hours, 
and may offer amenities such as restrooms and changing facilities. 
WHEREAS, resolution 2025-426 was adopted on May 21, 2025 setting the hours 
of parking at town beach lots, and the resolution that was adopted omitted the exception 
for vehicles with night fishing permits; and 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, This Town Board sets the hours for all 
public bathing beaches to be open weekends from May 24 to June 29 and open seven 
days a week from June 30 until, and including, Labor Day during the hours 11am until 
6pm.  
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, the Town Board hereby sets and 
establishes that the hours for parking of vehicles at Town Beach parking lots, with a 
valid Riverhead Town beach permit shall be between the hours of 6 a.m. and 10 p.m. 
daily, and that overnight parking of vehicles shall be prohibited except for vehicles with a 
valid fishing license properly displayed.  
BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain 
a copy of this resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified 
copy of same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
SECONDER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

06.03.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-509 
 
CLASSIFIES THE SPECIAL PERMIT AND SITE PLAN APPLICATIONS OF DUFFY 
MX MOTOCROSS TRACK AS A TYPE 1 ACTION PURSUANT TO SEQRA, 
REQUESTS LEAD AGENCY STATUS FOR THE PURPOSES OF COORDINATED 
REVIEW 2822 RIVER ROAD, CALVERTON, NY SCTM NO. 600-136-1-4 
 
Councilwoman Merrifield offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Waski 
 
WHEREAS, the Riverhead Town Board is in receipt of a Special Permit 
application, seeking approval to construct and operate an outdoor motocross race track 
facility upon land located at 2822 River Road, Calverton, located within the Calverton 
Industrial (CI) zoning use district, and more particularly described as SCTM No. 600 -
136-1-4; and  
 
 WHEREAS, a Special Permit from the Town Board is required for the 
construction and operation of an outdoor motocross race track in accordance with 
Riverhead Town Code §301-122, Attachment 4B; and  
 
 WHEREAS, the proposed action is a Type 1 action pursuant to 6NYCRR Part 
617.4(b)(6)(i), as it involves physical disturbance in excess of 10-aces, thereby requiring 
mandatory coordinated review among involved agencies; and  
 
WHEREAS, the following agencies are identified as being involved in the SEQR 
coordination process: 
 
1. Riverhead Planning Board. 
2. Riverhead Fire Marshal’s Office. 
3. Riverhead Water District. 
4. Suffolk County Planning Commission. 
5. Suffolk County Department of Health Services. 
6. Central Pine Barrens Commission. 
7. New York State Department of Environmental Conservation; and  
 
WHEREAS¸ the Town Board desires Lead Agency status for the purposes of 
SEQRA coordinated review.   
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED,  that the Town Board hereby classifies 
the Special Permit and Site Plan applications of Duffy MX Motocross Track as a Type 1 
action pursuant to SEQRA; and be it further 
 
 RESOLVED, that the Town Board hereby requests Lead Agency status for the 
purposes of coordinated SEQRA review; and be it further 
 
 RESOLVED, that upon the submission of an amended and corrected Full 
9.43
Packet Pg. 286
Environmental Assessment Form (FEAF), addressing all those issues identified in the 
Planning Department’s staff report, the Planning Department is hereby authorized to 
circulate a Lead Agency request to involved agencies on behalf of the Town Board; and 
be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby authorized to forward a certified copy 
of this resolution to Victor Prusinowski (vicspindoc@aol.com); and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.  
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
SECONDER: Joann Waski, Councilwoman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

expire December 30, 2025; and be it further,
